2026-03-13 11:01:49.433 +05:30 [INF] Executed DbCommand (18ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[SupplierId], [s].[Name], [p].[OrderDate], [p].[Status], [p].[TotalAmount], [s].[Id], [s0].[Id], [s0].[ProductId], [s0].[ProductName], [s0].[Quantity], [s0].[UnitCost], [s0].[Id0]
FROM [PurchaseOrders] AS [p]
INNER JOIN [Suppliers] AS [s] ON [p].[SupplierId] = [s].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[Id], [p0].[ProductId], [p1].[Name] AS [ProductName], [p0].[Quantity], [p0].[UnitCost], [p1].[Id] AS [Id0], [p0].[PurchaseOrderId]
    FROM [PurchaseOrderItems] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Products] AS [p1] ON [p0].[ProductId] = [p1].[Id]

SELECT TOP(@p) [s].[ProductId], [s].[Name0] AS [Name], COALESCE(SUM([s].[Quantity]), 0) AS [QuantitySold], COALESCE(SUM([s].[LineTotal]), 0.0) AS [Revenue]
FROM (
    SELECT [o].[LineTotal], [o].[ProductId], [o].[Quantity], [p].[Name] AS [Name0]
    FROM [OrderItems] AS [o]
    INNER JOIN [Products] AS [p] ON [o].[ProductId] = [p].[Id]
) AS [s]
GROUP BY [s].[ProductId], [s].[Name0]
ORDER BY COALESCE(SUM([s].[Quantity]), 0) DESC
